ALTER PROC [dbo].[UserLogin]   
 -- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here  
 @UserName varchar(max),  
 @Password varchar(max)
AS  
BEGIN  
 -- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from  
 -- interfering with SELECT statements.  
 SET NOCOUNT ON;  
  
    -- Insert statements for procedure here  
    DECLARE @Pwd AS VARCHAR(MAX)  
    DECLARE @Msg AS VARCHAR(MAX)  
      
    DECLARE @PROGNAME AS VARCHAR(MAX)  
    DECLARE @HOSTNAME AS VARCHAR(MAX)  
    DECLARE @IPADD AS VARCHAR(MAX)  
	DECLARE @LogDate AS VARCHAR(MAX)  
   
    SET @PROGNAME = (SELECT PROGRAM_NAME())  
    SET @HOSTNAME = (SELECT HOST_NAME())  
    SET @IPADD = (SELECT TOP 1 ISNULL(client_net_address,'') FROM sys.dm_exec_connections WHERE session_id=@@SPId)  
    SET @LogDate = (SELECT CAST(GETDATE() AS VARCHAR(MAX)))  
      
    IF @IPADD <> ''  
    BEGIN   
  
    IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT TOP 1 1 FROM USER_PC_LOG WHERE PROGNAME = @PROGNAME AND IPADD = @IPADD)  
    INSERT INTO USER_PC_LOG VALUES (@PROGNAME,@HOSTNAME,@IPADD,@LogDate)  
  
    END  
      
	OPEN SYMMETRIC KEY EncryptKey DECRYPTION BY CERTIFICATE EncryptCert  
   
	SET @Pwd =  isnull((SELECT top 1 CONVERT(NVARCHAR,DECRYPTBYKEY(EPWD)) AS Pwd  
    FROM Users2  
    WHERE (UserName = @UserName OR UserID = @UserName)),'12345')  
      
	CLOSE ALL SYMMETRIC KEYS  
   
	BEGIN    
    
 --SELECT top 1 i.UserID,i.UserName,i.Pwd,ISNULL(i.SapID,'')SapID,ISNULL(i.SapPwd,'')SapPwd,i.LisID,i.LisPwd,i.EmpID,i.EmpName,isnull(i.WhsCode,'')WhsCode,  
 --  isnull(i.Dept,'')Dept,isnull(i.Section,'')Section,i.UType,i.Stat,i.ReqUser,i.ReqPWD,i.BCODE,i.EndOIC,i.ManOIC,i.ReqUtype,i.EPwd,IsNull(i.SLPCode,'')SLPCode  
 --FROM Users2 i
 --INNER JOIN [192.171.11.7].[HPCOMMON].[dbo].SCEMP p on i.EmpID = p.EmpCode collate database_default
 --WHERE RTRIM(@Pwd) = RTRIM(@Password) AND (UserName = @UserName OR UserID = @UserName)  and isnull(p.DateResigned,'01/01/3000')  > Cast(getdate() as Date)  

	 --SELECT Top 1 UserID,UserName,Pwd,ISNULL(SapID,'')SapID,ISNULL(SapPwd,'')SapPwd,LisID,LisPwd,EmpID,EmpName,isnull(WhsCode,'')WhsCode,  
		--			isnull(Dept,'')Dept,isnull(Section,'')Section,UType,Stat,ReqUser,ReqPWD,BCODE,EndOIC,ManOIC,ReqUtype1,EPwd,IsNull(SLPCode,'')SLPCode,
		--			ISNULL((SELECT TOP 1 fname FROM ScEmp WHERE EmpCode=UserID),EmpName) Fname,ISNULL((SELECT TOP 1 seccode FROM ScEmp WHERE EmpCode=UserID),0)SEccode
	 --FROM Users2

	 SELECT Top 1 UserID,UserName,Pwd,ISNULL(SapID,'')SapID,ISNULL(SapPwd,'')SapPwd,LisID,LisPwd,EmpID,EmpName,
					--ISNULL(WhsCode,'')WhsCode,  
					ISNULL((SELECT TOP 1 WhsCode FROM ScEmp WHERE EmpCode=UserID),WhsCode) WhsCode,
					isnull(Dept,'')Dept,isnull(Section,'')Section,UType,Stat,ReqUser,ReqPWD,BCODE,EndOIC,ManOIC,ReqUtype1,EPwd,IsNull(SLPCode,'')SLPCode,
					ISNULL((SELECT TOP 1 fname FROM ScEmp WHERE EmpCode=UserID),EmpName) Fname,
					ISNULL((SELECT TOP 1 seccode FROM dbo.SCEmpNew WHERE EmpCode=UserID),0)Seccode
					,ISNULL((SELECT TOP 1 Deptcode FROM dbo.SCEmpNew WHERE EmpCode=UserID),0)Deptcode,'' Position
	 FROM Users2 
	 
	 WHERE RTRIM(@Pwd) = RTRIM(@Password) AND (UserName = @UserName OR UserID = @UserName)  and isnull(ResignDate,'01/01/4000') > Cast(getdate() as Date)  
  
	END  
END  
 


CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Users2](
	[UserID] [VARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[UserName] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[Pwd] [NVARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[SapID] [NVARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[SapPwd] [NVARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[LisID] [NVARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[LisPwd] [NVARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[EmpID] [VARCHAR](20) NOT NULL,
	[EmpName] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
	[WhsCode] [VARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[Dept] [VARCHAR](100) NULL,
	[Section] [VARCHAR](500) NULL,
	[UType] [VARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[Stat] [VARCHAR](10) NULL,
	[ReqUser] [VARCHAR](500) NULL,
	[ReqPWD] [VARCHAR](50) NULL,
	[BCODE] [VARCHAR](12) NULL,
	[EndOIC] [VARCHAR](10) NULL,
	[ManOIC] [VARCHAR](10) NULL,
	[EPwd] [VARBINARY](256) NULL,
	[SLPCode] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[AuthStat] [BIT] NULL,
	[PxDemoStat] [BIT] NULL,
	[OutLookSig] [VARCHAR](50) NULL,
	[AOPapp] [INT] NULL,
	[AOPCancel] [INT] NULL,
	[IMGSchedStat] [BIT] NULL,
	[ResignDate] [DATE] NULL,
	[ReqUtype1] [VARCHAR](100) NULL,
	[OutlookMail] [VARCHAR](100) NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_Users2] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[EmpID] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY] TEXTIMAGE_ON [PRIMARY]


CREATE TABLE #temptable ( [UserID] varchar(20), [UserName] varchar(30), [Pwd] nvarchar(20), [SapID] nvarchar(20), [SapPwd] nvarchar(20), [LisID] nvarchar(20), [LisPwd] nvarchar(20), [EmpID] varchar(20), [EmpName] varchar(max), [WhsCode] varchar(20), [Dept] varchar(100), [Section] varchar(500), [UType] varchar(20), [Stat] varchar(10), [ReqUser] varchar(500), [ReqPWD] varchar(50), [BCODE] varchar(12), [EndOIC] varchar(10), [ManOIC] varchar(10), [EPwd] varbinary(256), [SLPCode] varchar(30), [AuthStat] bit, [PxDemoStat] bit, [OutLookSig] varchar(50), [AOPapp] int, [AOPCancel] int, [IMGSchedStat] bit, [ResignDate] date, [ReqUtype1] varchar(100), [OutlookMail] varchar(100) )
